<section id="content" style="width: 100%;">
					<div id="post-23071" class="post-23071 page type-page status-publish hentry">
			
			
			<div class="post-content">
				<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-1 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;--awb-flex-wrap:wrap;"><div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start fusion-flex-justify-content-center fusion-flex-content-wrap" style="max-width:1248px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );"><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-0 fusion_builder_column_2_3 2_3 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:66.666666666667%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:2.88%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:2.88%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-1" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><h2><b>Our Little Giving Artists Pay Forward in support of National Day 2022</b></h2>
<p>Following the success of our Little Giving Artists fund raising effort in 2021, the Skool4Kidz Preschoolers are at it again! In conjunction with National Day 2022, our children created more art pieces for sale to continue the support of worthy causes. This time, to benefit other children with developmental needs in our midst!</p>
<p>Little Giving Artists is a community outreach project by Skool4Kidz Preschoolers to pay forward. Supported by Skool4Kidz Corporate Social Responsibility arm, namely Skool4Kidz Care Fund, all proceeds will be donated via Giving.SG to support those who are in need. This outreach effort inculcates compassion and selflessness in our little ones while showcasing their artistic creativity and prowess. This year, our children will support other children with development difficulties in their inclusive early years’ learning.</p>
</div><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-2" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p>This Skool4Kidz Care Fund community outreach initiative is in commemoration of National Day 2022. We are indeed <b>Stronger Together, Majulah!</b></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-1 fusion_builder_column_1_3 1_3 fusion-flex-column" class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div style="text-align:center;"><a class="fusion-button button-flat Gallery</span></a></div><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-3"><p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-21674 lazyautosizes ls-is-cached lazyloaded" class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-4" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p>All proceeds from the art pieces hand-painted by our preschoolers will be matched dollar-for-dollar by the Skool4Kidz Care Fund and donated to <a href="https://www.awwa.org.sg/our-services/6-months-to-6-years-old/kindle-garden-preschool/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">AWWA’s Kindle Garden (KG)</a>. KG is Singapore’s first inclusive preschool for children of all abilities. The funds raised will go towards KG’s purchase of indoor gym materials and equipment to support their children’s gross motor development.</p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-4 fusion_builder_column_1_3 1_3 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p>Our Kindergarten 1 and 2 children personally created close to 170 hand-painted art pieces with the theme of ‘QR Code and I’. The theme expresses our children’s experience with Technology Empowerment through visual art. Our In-Centre Art Enrichment programme specialist teachers from <u><a href="https://crestar.com.sg/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Crestar </a><a href="https://crestar.com.sg/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Learning</a><a href="https://crestar.com.sg/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"> Centre</a></u> are on hand to guide our children to create the art pieces using various mediums, including acrylic paint on canvas.</p>

class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-6" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p>All the creations by our Little Giving Artists are showcased in Skool4Kidz Preschools’ online art gallery from 24 June 2022. Donations at a minimum sum of $30 were collected through <a href="https://www.giving.sg/campaigns/Skool4Kidz_LittleGivingArtists_2022" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Giving.sg</span></a>. For this sum, the donors can bring home an art piece selected from the Skool4Kidz Preschools’ online art gallery and also receive a personalised message from our Little Giving Artists. The donation drive has ended in July 2022.</p>
</div><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-7" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p>Every dollar raised from the donation will be matched dollar-for-dollar by the Skool4Kidz Care Fund in support of this meaningful campaign by our preschoolers. KG is the sole beneficiary of this fundraising outreach and 100% of the gross donation will benefit KG in support of their children with developmental needs.</p>
<p><b>*Donations are eligible for 250% personal income tax deduction, administered by giving.sg.</b></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-8 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-8" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><h4 style="text-align: center; font-size: 21px;"><strong>Thank you for the kind support, this community outreach initiative has ended.</strong></h4>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-9 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><script src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-1.12.4.min.js"></script>
<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    var url = new URL(window.location); // Construct URL object using current browser URL
    var params = url.searchParams; // Get query parameters object
    var S4Kcentre = params.get("S4Kcentre"); // Get value of S4Kcentre
    $("#S4Kcentre").val(S4Kcentre); // Set it as the dropdown value
    $("select").change(function(){
        $(this).find("option:selected").each(function(){
            var optionValue = $(this).attr("value");
            window.history.replaceState(null, null, "?S4Kcentre=" + optionValue);
            if(optionValue){
                $(".centre").not("." + optionValue).hide();
                $("." + optionValue).show();
            }
        });
    }).change();
});
</script><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-9" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><p style="text-align: center;"><select id="S4Kcentre" name="S4Kcentre"><option value="SKC">SKOOL4KIDZ CAMPUS @ SENGKANG RIVERSIDE PARK (SKC)</option><option value="SBEC">SKOOL4KIDZ PRESCHOOL @ SEMBAWANG EAST CROWN (SBEC)</option><option value="WLCM">SKOOL4KIDZ PRESCHOOL @ WOODLANDS CRESCENT (WLCM)</option><option value="WLRR">SKOOL4KIDZ PRESCHOOL @ WOODLANDS RING ROAD (WLRR)</option><option value="YSOB">SKOOL4KIDZ PRESCHOOL @ YISHUN OLEANDER BREEZE (YSOB)</option><option value="YSOS">SKOOL4KIDZ PRESCHOOL @ YISHUN ORCHID SPRING (YSOS)</option></select></p>
